<p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 17px; letter-spacing: 0.544px; text-align: justify; widows: 1; line-height: 25.5px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">
	<span style="font-size:18px;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 楷体; line-height: 24px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">&nbsp;</span></span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 17px; letter-spacing: 0.544px; text-align: justify; widows: 1; line-height: 25.5px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">
	<span style="font-size:18px;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 楷体; line-height: 24px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">画成图表，则更加直观一点。</span></span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 17px; letter-spacing: 0.544px; text-align: justify; widows: 1; line-height: 25.5px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">
	<span style="font-size:18px;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 楷体; line-height: 24px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">实线是</span>“零首付流”，虚线是“笋盘流”。</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 楷体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">&nbsp;</span></span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 17px; letter-spacing: 0.544px; line-height: 27.2px; text-align: justify; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">
	<img alt="" src="/uploads/180820/1-1PR0103224J0.jpg" style="width: 100%; height: 375px;"></p>
<p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 17px; letter-spacing: 0.544px; text-align: justify; widows: 1; line-height: 25.5px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">
	<span style="font-size:18px;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 楷体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">“笋盘流”几乎一直都在盈利线以上。</span></span></p>
<blockquote style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px 0px 0px 10px; max-width: 100%; border-left: 3px solid rgb(219, 219, 219); color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 17px; letter-spacing: 0.544px; line-height: 27.2px; text-align: justify; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">
	<p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; clear: both; min-height: 1em; line-height: 1.75em;">
		<span style="font-size:18px;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 微软雅黑; line-height: 31.5px; color: rgb(0, 0, 255); box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">三年涨</span>+40%，或者五年涨+64%以上，</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; color: rgb(0, 0, 255); font-family: 微软雅黑; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">则笋盘流被“零首付流”收</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; color: rgb(0, 0, 255); font-family: 微软雅黑; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">益超出。</span></span></p>
</blockquote>
<p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 17px; letter-spacing: 0.544px; text-align: justify; widows: 1; line-height: 25.5px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">
	<span style="font-size:18px;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 楷体; line-height: 24px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">&nbsp;</span></span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 17px; letter-spacing: 0.544px; text-align: justify; widows: 1; line-height: 25.5px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">
	<span style="font-size:18px;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 楷体; line-height: 24px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">&nbsp;</span></span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 17px; letter-spacing: 0.544px; text-align: justify; widows: 1; line-height: 25.5px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">
	<span style="font-size:18px;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 楷体; line-height: 24px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">哥哥盯着这个图表，左看右看，左看右看了半天，最后得出一个结论。你知道是什么：</span></span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 17px; letter-spacing: 0.544px; text-align: justify; widows: 1; line-height: 25.5px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">
	<span style="font-size:18px;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 楷体; line-height: 27px; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">“零首付流”毫无价值。</span></span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 17px; letter-spacing: 0.544px; text-align: justify; widows: 1; line-height: 25.5px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">
	<span style="font-size:18px;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 楷体; line-height: 24px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">&nbsp;</span></span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 17px; letter-spacing: 0.544px; text-align: justify; widows: 1; line-height: 25.5px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">
	<span style="font-size:18px;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 楷体; line-height: 24px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">为什么，因为你看看这个图表。</span>“笋盘流”已经非常完美了。</span></span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 17px; letter-spacing: 0.544px; text-align: justify; widows: 1; line-height: 25.5px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">
	<span style="font-size:18px;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 楷体; line-height: 24px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">以三年计算，笋盘流已经提供了</span>+20%年复合回报。</span></span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 17px; letter-spacing: 0.544px; text-align: justify; widows: 1; line-height: 25.5px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">
	<span style="font-size:18px;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 楷体; line-height: 24px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">作为</span>“稳健投资”，每年有+20%很不错了。</span></span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 17px; letter-spacing: 0.544px; text-align: justify; widows: 1; line-height: 25.5px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">
	<span style="font-size:18px;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 楷体; line-height: 24px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">&nbsp;</span></span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 17px; letter-spacing: 0.544px; text-align: justify; widows: 1; line-height: 25.5px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">
	<span style="font-size:18px;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 楷体; line-height: 24px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">&nbsp;</span></span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 17px; letter-spacing: 0.544px; text-align: justify; widows: 1; line-height: 25.5px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">
	<span style="font-size:18px;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 楷体; line-height: 24px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">而</span>“零首付流”要到三年涨幅+40%之后，收益才能反超。</span></span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 17px; letter-spacing: 0.544px; text-align: justify; widows: 1; line-height: 25.5px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">
	<span style="font-size:18px;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 楷体; line-height: 24px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">之前一直是巨额亏损。</span></span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 17px; letter-spacing: 0.544px; text-align: justify; widows: 1; line-height: 25.5px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">
	<span style="font-size:18px;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 楷体; line-height: 24px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">亏损，呃，俺不能接受亏损。</span></span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 17px; letter-spacing: 0.544px; text-align: justify; widows: 1; line-height: 25.5px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">
	<span style="font-size:18px;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 楷体; line-height: 24px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">&nbsp;</span></span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 17px; letter-spacing: 0.544px; text-align: justify; widows: 1; line-height: 25.5px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">
	<span style="font-size:18px;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 楷体; line-height: 24px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">对于绝大多数的投资者而言，收益率</span>+40%以后，+60%还是横财，带来快乐有限。</span></span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 17px; letter-spacing: 0.544px; text-align: justify; widows: 1; line-height: 25.5px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">
	<span style="font-size:18px;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 楷体; line-height: 24px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">而亏损的</span>“巨额风险”绝对不可以接受的。</span></span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 17px; letter-spacing: 0.544px; text-align: justify; widows: 1; line-height: 25.5px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">
	<span style="font-size:18px;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 楷体; line-height: 24px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">&nbsp;</span></span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 17px; letter-spacing: 0.544px; text-align: justify; widows: 1; line-height: 25.5px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">
	<span style="font-size:18px;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 楷体; line-height: 24px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">&nbsp;</span></span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 17px; letter-spacing: 0.544px; text-align: justify; widows: 1; line-height: 25.5px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">
	<span style="font-size:18px;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 楷体; line-height: 24px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">从风险喜好角度，是不是该把</span>“零首付流”给毙了。</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 楷体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">&nbsp;</span></span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 17px; letter-spacing: 0.544px; line-height: 27.2px; text-align: justify; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">
	<span style="font-size:18px;"><img alt="" src="/uploads/180820/1-1PR010324JW.jpg" style="width: 100%; height: 467px;"></span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 17px; letter-spacing: 0.544px; text-align: justify; widows: 1; line-height: 25.5px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">
	<span style="font-size:18px;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 楷体; line-height: 19.5px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">（在</span>8.18的影居活动中，罗尼大声呼吁，“零首付流”过度进取，风险重重。她说得对不对？）</span></span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 17px; letter-spacing: 0.544px; text-align: justify; widows: 1; line-height: 25.5px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">
	&nbsp;</p>
<p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 17px; letter-spacing: 0.544px; text-align: justify; widows: 1; line-height: 25.5px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">
	<span style="font-size:18px;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 楷体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">五）</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 楷体; line-height: 24px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">超短期</span></span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 17px; letter-spacing: 0.544px; text-align: justify; widows: 1; line-height: 25.5px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">
	<span style="font-size:18px;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 楷体; line-height: 24px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">&nbsp;</span></span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 17px; letter-spacing: 0.544px; text-align: justify; widows: 1; line-height: 25.5px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">
	<span style="font-size:18px;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 楷体; line-height: 24px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">哥哥手贱，我又测算了一个</span>“一年期”的回报率。</span></span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 17px; letter-spacing: 0.544px; text-align: justify; widows: 1; line-height: 25.5px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">
	<span style="font-size:18px;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 楷体; line-height: 24px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">然后我默默给自己写了四个字：</span>“以上全错”。</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 楷体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">&nbsp;</span></span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 17px; letter-spacing: 0.544px; line-height: 27.2px; text-align: justify; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">
	<span style="font-size:18px;"><img alt="" src="/uploads/180820/1-1PR0103313L0.jpg" style="width: 100%; height: 373px;"></span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 17px; letter-spacing: 0.544px; text-align: justify; widows: 1; line-height: 25.5px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">
	<span style="font-size:18px;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 楷体; line-height: 24px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">真的是，令人印象深刻的</span>…………超级曲线啊。</span></span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 17px; letter-spacing: 0.544px; text-align: justify; widows: 1; line-height: 25.5px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">
	<span style="font-size:18px;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 楷体; line-height: 24px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">“零首付流”的回报曲线，一骑绝尘，远远向着4000%走去了。</span></span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 17px; letter-spacing: 0.544px; text-align: justify; widows: 1; line-height: 25.5px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">
	<span style="font-size:18px;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 楷体; line-height: 24px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">&nbsp;</span></span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 17px; letter-spacing: 0.544px; text-align: justify; widows: 1; line-height: 25.5px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">
	&nbsp;</p>
<p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 17px; letter-spacing: 0.544px; text-align: justify; widows: 1; line-height: 25.5px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">
	<span style="font-size:18px;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 楷体; line-height: 24px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">我们之前看</span>“三年期，五年期”的回报率比较，“零首付流”并没有特别优势。</span></span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 17px; letter-spacing: 0.544px; text-align: justify; widows: 1; line-height: 25.5px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">
	<span style="font-size:18px;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 楷体; line-height: 24px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">因为零首付也要付月供，三年填进去了</span>27%的房款。</span></span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 17px; letter-spacing: 0.544px; text-align: justify; widows: 1; line-height: 25.5px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">
	<span style="font-size:18px;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 楷体; line-height: 24px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">&nbsp;</span></span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 17px; letter-spacing: 0.544px; text-align: justify; widows: 1; line-height: 25.5px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">
	<span style="font-size:18px;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 楷体; line-height: 24px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">但是</span>“一年期”的比较，则非常惊人。甚至远远打爆了表格的上限。</span></span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 17px; letter-spacing: 0.544px; text-align: justify; widows: 1; line-height: 25.5px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">
	<span style="font-size:18px;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 楷体; line-height: 24px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">在整个标量中，最重要的真是</span>“时间”。</span></span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 17px; letter-spacing: 0.544px; text-align: justify; widows: 1; line-height: 25.5px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">
	<span style="font-size:18px;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 楷体; line-height: 24px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">&nbsp;</span></span></p>
<blockquote style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px 0px 0px 10px; max-width: 100%; border-left: 3px solid rgb(219, 219, 219); color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 17px; letter-spacing: 0.544px; line-height: 27.2px; text-align: justify; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">
	<p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; clear: both; min-height: 1em; line-height: 25.5px;">
		<span style="font-size:18px;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 微软雅黑; line-height: 31.5px; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">如果你追求短期快涨，大涨前夜。则应该追求杠杆。</span></span></p>
	<p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; clear: both; min-height: 1em; line-height: 25.5px;">
		<span style="font-size:18px;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 微软雅黑; line-height: 31.5px; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">如果你持有时间较长，则应该追求笋盘。</span></span></p>
</blockquote>
<p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 17px; letter-spacing: 0.544px; text-align: justify; widows: 1; line-height: 25.5px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">
	<span style="font-size:18px;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 楷体; line-height: 24px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">&nbsp;</span></span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 17px; letter-spacing: 0.544px; text-align: justify; widows: 1; line-height: 25.5px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">
	<span style="font-size:18px;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 楷体; line-height: 24px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">关于</span>“杠杆和笋盘”的争议，最应该问的，是你预期要持有多少年。</span></span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 17px; letter-spacing: 0.544px; text-align: justify; widows: 1; line-height: 25.5px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">
	<span style="font-size:18px;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 楷体; line-height: 24px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">越是确定在</span>“大涨前夜”，而且涨了就可以抛现，一年以内，就应该选择杠杆。</span></span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 17px; letter-spacing: 0.544px; text-align: justify; widows: 1; line-height: 25.5px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">
	<span style="font-size:18px;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 楷体; line-height: 24px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">&nbsp;</span></span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 17px; letter-spacing: 0.544px; text-align: justify; widows: 1; line-height: 25.5px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">
	<span style="font-size:18px;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 楷体; line-height: 24px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">&nbsp;</span></span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 17px; letter-spacing: 0.544px; text-align: justify; widows: 1; line-height: 25.5px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">
	<span style="font-size:18px;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 楷体; line-height: 24px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">众所周知，<a href="http://www.shuikult.net/" target="_blank"><u>水库</u></a>的主要手法是</span>“大面积，低单价”。而且流派倾向于长持为主。</span></span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 17px; letter-spacing: 0.544px; text-align: justify; widows: 1; line-height: 25.5px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">
	<span style="font-size:18px;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 楷体; line-height: 24px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">我们去到一个新的城市，往往会期待一个十年的雪坡。</span></span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 17px; letter-spacing: 0.544px; text-align: justify; widows: 1; line-height: 25.5px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">
	<span style="font-size:18px;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 楷体; line-height: 24px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">水库主要的审美观，还是侧重</span>“淘笋”，而不是“拼命加杠杆”。</span></span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 17px; letter-spacing: 0.544px; text-align: justify; widows: 1; line-height: 25.5px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">
	<span style="font-size:18px;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 楷体; line-height: 24px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">&nbsp;</span></span></p>
<blockquote style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px 0px 0px 10px; max-width: 100%; border-left: 3px solid rgb(219, 219, 219); color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 17px; letter-spacing: 0.544px; line-height: 27.2px; text-align: justify; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">
	<p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; clear: both; min-height: 1em; line-height: 25.5px;">
		<span style="font-size:18px;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; line-height: 18px; color: rgb(197, 89, 17); box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">蓝色水库：亲，我有一个问题咨询你。</span></span></p>
	<p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; clear: both; min-height: 1em; line-height: 25.5px;">
		<span style="font-size:18px;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; line-height: 18px; color: rgb(197, 89, 17); box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">蓝色水库：同一个小区有二种车位，一个价格</span>16W。一个价格32W，但可以贷款50%。请问哪种好。</span></span></p>
	<p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; clear: both; min-height: 1em; line-height: 25.5px;">
		<span style="font-size:18px;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; line-height: 18px; color: rgb(197, 89, 17); box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">Yevon_ou：…………</span></span></p>
</blockquote>
<p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 17px; letter-spacing: 0.544px; text-align: justify; widows: 1; line-height: 25.5px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">
	<span style="font-size:18px;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 楷体; line-height: 24px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">&nbsp;</span></span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 17px; letter-spacing: 0.544px; text-align: justify; widows: 1; line-height: 25.5px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">
	<span style="font-size:18px;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 楷体; line-height: 24px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">&nbsp;</span></span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 17px; letter-spacing: 0.544px; text-align: justify; widows: 1; line-height: 25.5px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">
	<span style="font-size:18px;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 楷体; line-height: 24px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">&nbsp;</span></span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 17px; letter-spacing: 0.544px; text-align: justify; widows: 1; line-height: 25.5px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">
	<span style="font-size:18px;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 楷体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">六）</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 楷体; line-height: 24px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">关于风险的把控</span></span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 17px; letter-spacing: 0.544px; text-align: justify; widows: 1; line-height: 25.5px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">
	<span style="font-size:18px;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 楷体; line-height: 24px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">&nbsp;</span></span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 17px; letter-spacing: 0.544px; text-align: justify; widows: 1; line-height: 25.5px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">
	<span style="font-size:18px;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 楷体; line-height: 24px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">对于风险，我想很多人都误解一件事。</span></span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 17px; letter-spacing: 0.544px; text-align: justify; widows: 1; line-height: 25.5px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">
	<span style="font-size:18px;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 楷体; line-height: 24px; color: rgb(0, 0, 255); box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">所有的风险，都是边际风险。</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 楷体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">&nbsp;</span></span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 17px; letter-spacing: 0.544px; text-align: justify; widows: 1; line-height: 25.5px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">
	<span style="font-size:18px;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 楷体; line-height: 24px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">&nbsp;</span></span></p>
<blockquote style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px 0px 0px 10px; max-width: 100%; border-left: 3px solid rgb(219, 219, 219); color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 17px; letter-spacing: 0.544px; line-height: 27.2px; text-align: justify; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">
	<p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; clear: both; min-height: 1em; line-height: 25.5px;">
		<span style="font-size:18px;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 楷体; line-height: 22.5px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">譬如说，一个人有2000W净资产。然后他跑到CQ，全款“零首付”买了一套房子。</span></span></p>
	<p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; clear: both; min-height: 1em; line-height: 25.5px;">
		<span style="font-size:18px;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 楷体; line-height: 22.5px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">你说他“风险”么。CQ人都要吓傻掉了。日夜担心。</span></span></p>
	<p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; clear: both; min-height: 1em; line-height: 25.5px;">
		<span style="font-size:18px;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 楷体; line-height: 22.5px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">&nbsp;</span></span></p>
	<p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; clear: both; min-height: 1em; line-height: 25.5px;">
		<span style="font-size:18px;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 楷体; line-height: 22.5px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">但是你说“安全”么，对于一个有2000W净资产的人来说，多加一套80W的房子，算什么风险。</span></span></p>
	<p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; clear: both; min-height: 1em; line-height: 25.5px;">
		<span style="font-size:18px;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 楷体; line-height: 22.5px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">&nbsp;</span></span></p>
	<p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; clear: both; min-height: 1em; line-height: 25.5px;">
		<span style="font-size:18px;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 楷体; line-height: 22.5px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">哪怕他少付了24W首付，说不定他自己的主力仓位。三个月月供就十几万了呢。这半年下来，总负债还是减少的呢。</span></span></p>
</blockquote>
<p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 17px; letter-spacing: 0.544px; text-align: justify; widows: 1; line-height: 25.5px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">
	<span style="font-size:18px;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 楷体; line-height: 24px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">&nbsp;</span></span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 17px; letter-spacing: 0.544px; text-align: justify; widows: 1; line-height: 25.5px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">
	<span style="font-size:18px;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 楷体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">&nbsp;</span></span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 17px; letter-spacing: 0.544px; text-align: justify; widows: 1; line-height: 25.5px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">
	<span style="font-size:18px;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 楷体; line-height: 24px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">对于绝大多数人来说，他的</span>“底仓”是不动的。京沪深大型的，高价值的物业，想动也没法动。</span></span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 17px; letter-spacing: 0.544px; text-align: justify; widows: 1; line-height: 25.5px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">
	<span style="font-size:18px;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 楷体; line-height: 24px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">&nbsp;</span></span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 17px; letter-spacing: 0.544px; text-align: justify; widows: 1; line-height: 25.5px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">
	<span style="font-size:18px;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 楷体; line-height: 24px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">“不动如山”。如果你90%的仓位，都是稳岻如山岳的。</span></span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 17px; letter-spacing: 0.544px; text-align: justify; widows: 1; line-height: 25.5px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">
	<span style="font-size:18px;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 楷体; line-height: 24px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">那么你</span>10%的先头部队，刀磨得再快，又有什么关系呢。</span></span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 17px; letter-spacing: 0.544px; text-align: justify; widows: 1; line-height: 25.5px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">
	<span style="font-size:18px;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 楷体; line-height: 24px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">&nbsp;</span></span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 17px; letter-spacing: 0.544px; text-align: justify; widows: 1; line-height: 25.5px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">
	<span style="font-size:18px;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 楷体; line-height: 24px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">几乎所有的多军，都缺乏现金。而自己的债务，每个月都在减轻。</span></span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 17px; letter-spacing: 0.544px; text-align: justify; widows: 1; line-height: 25.5px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">
	<span style="font-size:18px;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 楷体; line-height: 24px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">把少量</span>“高能”的先头部队，磨得尖锐一点，又有什么关系呢。</span></span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 17px; letter-spacing: 0.544px; text-align: justify; widows: 1; line-height: 25.5px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">
	<span style="font-size:18px;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 楷体; line-height: 24px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">&nbsp;</span></span></p>
<blockquote style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px 0px 0px 10px; max-width: 100%; border-left: 3px solid rgb(219, 219, 219); color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 17px; letter-spacing: 0.544px; line-height: 27.2px; text-align: justify; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">
	<p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; clear: both; min-height: 1em; line-height: 25.5px;">
		<span style="font-size:18px;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 楷体; line-height: 24px; color: rgb(0, 0, 255); box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">你看到的全力一刀，其实并不是全力一刀</span></span></p>
</blockquote>
<p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 17px; letter-spacing: 0.544px; text-align: justify; widows: 1; line-height: 25.5px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">
	<span style="font-size:18px;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 楷体; line-height: 24px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">&nbsp;</span></span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 17px; letter-spacing: 0.544px; text-align: justify; widows: 1; line-height: 25.5px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">
	<span style="font-size:18px;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 楷体; line-height: 24px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">对于我们来说，</span>“锐刀”亦无非一种财务工具而已。</span></span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 17px; letter-spacing: 0.544px; text-align: justify; widows: 1; line-height: 25.5px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">
	<span style="font-size:18px;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 楷体; line-height: 24px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">你肯不肯多出</span>10%的手续费，“借900W，还1000W”。</span></span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 17px; letter-spacing: 0.544px; text-align: justify; widows: 1; line-height: 25.5px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">
	<span style="font-size:18px;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 楷体; line-height: 24px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">&nbsp;</span></span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 17px; letter-spacing: 0.544px; text-align: justify; widows: 1; line-height: 25.5px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">
	<span style="font-size:18px;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 楷体; line-height: 24px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">类似的决策，是与否，唯一的影响因子，也仅仅是数学。</span></span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 17px; letter-spacing: 0.544px; text-align: justify; widows: 1; line-height: 25.5px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">
	<span style="font-size:18px;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 楷体; line-height: 24px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">和道德无关。</span></span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 17px; letter-spacing: 0.544px; text-align: justify; widows: 1; line-height: 25.5px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">
	<span style="font-size:18px;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 楷体; line-height: 24px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">&nbsp;</span></span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 17px; letter-spacing: 0.544px; text-align: justify; widows: 1; line-height: 25.5px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">
	<span style="font-size:18px;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 楷体; line-height: 24px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">&nbsp;</span></span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 17px; letter-spacing: 0.544px; text-align: justify; widows: 1; line-height: 25.5px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">
	<span style="font-size:18px;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 楷体; line-height: 24px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">你的父辈们，连贷款都没见过。背一点点贷款，吓得夜不能寐。</span></span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 17px; letter-spacing: 0.544px; text-align: justify; widows: 1; line-height: 25.5px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">
	<span style="font-size:18px;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 楷体; line-height: 24px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">但经历过的人都知道，这都是很小，很安全的事。</span></span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 17px; letter-spacing: 0.544px; text-align: justify; widows: 1; line-height: 25.5px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">
	<span style="font-size:18px;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 楷体; line-height: 24px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">&nbsp;</span></span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 17px; letter-spacing: 0.544px; text-align: justify; widows: 1; line-height: 25.5px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">
	<span style="font-size:18px;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 楷体; line-height: 24px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">没有坐过云霄飞车的小孩子，不用惊吓的哇哇大叫。</span></span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 17px; letter-spacing: 0.544px; text-align: justify; widows: 1; line-height: 25.5px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">
	<span style="font-size:18px;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 楷体; line-height: 24px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">&nbsp;</span></span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 17px; letter-spacing: 0.544px; text-align: justify; widows: 1; line-height: 25.5px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">
	<span style="font-size:18px;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 楷体; line-height: 24px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">&nbsp;</span></span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 17px; letter-spacing: 0.544px; text-align: justify; widows: 1; line-height: 25.5px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">
	<span style="font-size:18px;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 楷体; line-height: 24px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">&nbsp;</span></span></p>

	<span style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont;">水库微信大群，目前是从1群到37群。 一群又称 元老院。主要是论坛元老在里面。目前可有名额的可免费加入的只有37群。大群免费。原则上每个人只能加一个大群。已经在水库各大群的，请不要再次加群，以节省群资源。请直接添加徽信（mtsk09）或者识别扫描下方二维码添加。</span><br style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; zoom: 1; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont; word-wrap: break-word;">
